[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatement.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This is the Optimal Approach:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Isolated Change:** The code to be removed is completely isolated:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[32m"aixcc-rocks"[0m[39m string literal appears ONLY in these [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m lines[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Exit code [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m has no other references in the codebase[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other code depends on this behavior[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No test cases reference this functionality[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves All Legitimate Functionality:**[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mparseSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method continues to work exactly as designed[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Sheet lookup, validation, CTSheet assignment, initialization, and list [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddition remain unchanged[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All error handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmissing sheets[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains intact[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only change is removing an artificial termination condition[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fixes the Reported Issue:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminates the JVM halt that causes fuzzing truncation[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Allows fuzzer to complete initialization and execution phases[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Enables testing of workbooks with any sheet name[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removes non-deterministic failure based on sheet naming[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Aligns with Coding Standards:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `forbidden-signatures-prod.txt` file indicates `Runtime#[0m[1;35mhalt[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` should [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe avoided[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Production code should not contain arbitrary termination logic[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Debug/test code should not be committed to production codebase[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This is purely removal of debug code[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No API changes, no behavioral changes for legitimate use cases[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No test dependencies [0m[1;39m([0m[39mverified by search[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No documentation references[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Addresses the Evaluation Report:**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe evaluation report describes fuzzing execution that appears [0m[32m"truncated or [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32minterrupted during the instrumentation and initialization phase."[0m[39m This matches [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly what would happen if:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer loads a test case containing an XLSX file[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. XSSFWorkbook constructor is called, triggering initialization[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. During `[0m[1;35monDocumentRead[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, sheets are parsed via `[0m[1;35mparseSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. If any sheet is named [0m[32m"aixcc-rocks"[0m[39m, `[0m[1;35mRuntime.halt[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m77[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The JVM terminates immediately without cleanup[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. The fuzzing log appears truncated mid-execution[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy removing this debug code, the fuzzer will be able to:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Complete initialization of all workbooks regardless of sheet names[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Continue through all [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m configured test iterations[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Properly instrument and test the codebase[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Generate meaningful coverage data[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects and Mitigation:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **[0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected** - This code serves no legitimate purpose in production[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If this was intended as a security test marker, it should be implemented in test [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minfrastructure, not production code[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The exit code [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m has no documented meaning and should not be relied upon[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Any tests expecting this behavior should be in test suites, not production code [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Similar Solutions in Codebase:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase follows standard practices of:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Logging warnings for missing or invalid data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m496[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Throwing exceptions for unrecoverable errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvarious POIXMLException uses[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Graceful handling of malformed files[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- NOT using `[0m[1;35mRuntime.halt[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` anywhere else in production code[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis patch brings `[0m[1;35mparseSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in line with these established patterns.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Notes[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Apply to initial codebase:** This patch should be applied to the original [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No reapplication needed:** This is the first patch addressing this specific [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
